Using Agda 2.5.4 with the reference https://mroman42.github.io/ctlc/agda-hott/Total.html

## Requirements

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Agda has a pragma to work with HoTT:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="339" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="343" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="351" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="363" class="Symbol">#-}</a>
<a id="367" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="372" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="379" href="Agda.Primitive.html" class="Module">Agda.Primitive</a> <a id="394" class="Keyword">public</a>

<a id="402" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#402" class="Function">_</a> <a id="404" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="406" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="410" class="Comment">-- trick for avoiding Agda module errors (jekyll)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Universes
Type universe hierarchy. It hides Agda primitive
hierarchy and the keyword Set. It uses Type instead.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="602" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Universes"></a><a id="609" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#609" class="Module">Universes</a> <a id="619" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="628" class="Comment">-- Our Universe hierarchy. It is implemented over the primitive</a>
  <a id="694" class="Comment">-- Agda universe hierarchy but it uses Type instead of Set, the</a>
  <a id="760" class="Comment">-- usual name for the Universe in Agda.</a>
  <a id="Universes.Type"></a><a id="802" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="807" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="809" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="810" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#810" class="Bound">ℓ</a> <a id="812" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="814" href="Agda.Primitive.html#408" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="819" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="821" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="823" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="827" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="828" href="Agda.Primitive.html#627" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="833" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#810" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="834" class="Symbol">)</a>

## Empty Type

The empty type, representing falsehood.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="1186" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Empty"></a><a id="1193" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1193" class="Module">Empty</a> <a id="1199" class="Keyword">where</a>

    <a id="1268" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Empty.⊥"></a><a id="1273" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1273" class="Datatype">⊥</a> <a id="1275" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1276" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1276" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="1278" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="1280" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1282" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="1287" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1276" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="1290" class="Keyword">where</a>

    <a id="1301" class="Comment">-- Ex falso quodlibet</a>
    <a id="Empty.exfalso"></a><a id="1327" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1327" class="Function">exfalso</a> <a id="1335" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1337" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="1339" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1339" class="Bound">ℓ</a> <a id="1341" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1341" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="1343" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="1345" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1346" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1346" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="1348" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1350" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="1355" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1339" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="1356" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="1358" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1360" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1273" class="Datatype">⊥</a> <a id="1362" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1363" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1341" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="1365" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="1367" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1369" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1346" class="Bound">A</a>

## Unit

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="1506" class="Comment">-- Unit.  A type with a single element, representing truth.</a>
<a id="1566" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Unit"></a><a id="1573" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1573" class="Module">Unit</a> <a id="1578" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1579" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1579" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="1580" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="1582" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="1591" class="Comment">-- A record without fields is the unit type with a single</a>
  <a id="1651" class="Comment">-- constructor.</a>
  <a id="1669" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="Unit.⊤"></a><a id="1676" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1676" class="Record">⊤</a> <a id="1678" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1680" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="1685" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1579" class="Bound">ℓ</a> <a id="1687" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="1697" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="Unit.⊤.★"></a><a id="1709" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1709" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>

## Other basic types

Basic types of Martin-Löf type theory and some basic
functions.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="1834" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Basic"></a><a id="1841" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1841" class="Module">Basic</a> <a id="1847" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="1856" class="Comment">-- Sigma types are a particular case of records, but records can be</a>
  <a id="1926" class="Comment">-- constructed using only sigma types. Note that l ⊔ q is the maximum</a>
  <a id="1998" class="Comment">-- of two hierarchy levels l and q. This way, we define sigma types in</a>
  <a id="2071" class="Comment">-- full generality, at each universe.</a>
  <a id="2111" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="Basic.Σ"></a><a id="2118" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2118" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="2120" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2121" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2121" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="2124" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2124" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="2126" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2128" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2129" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2129" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="2131" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2133" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="2138" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2121" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="2140" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="2142" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2142" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="2144" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2146" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2129" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="2148" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2150" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="2155" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2124" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="2157" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2159" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2161" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="2166" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2167" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2121" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="2170" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="2172" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2124" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="2174" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2176" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="2186" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="Basic.Σ._,_"></a><a id="2198" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2198" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>

  <a id="2246" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="2251" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2118" class="Module">Σ</a> <a id="2253" class="Keyword">public</a>

  <a id="2263" class="Comment">-- Product type as a particular case of the sigma</a>
  <a id="Basic._×_"></a><a id="2315" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2315" class="Function Operator">_×_</a> <a id="2319" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2321" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="2323" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2323" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="2326" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2326" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="2328" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2330" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2331" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2331" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="2333" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2335" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="2340" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2323" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="2342" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2344" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2345" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2345" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="2347" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2349" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="2354" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2326" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="2356" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2358" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2360" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="2365" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2366" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2323" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="2369" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="2371" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2326" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="2373" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="2377" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2377" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2379" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2315" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="2381" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2381" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2383" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2385" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2118" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="2387" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2377" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2389" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="2392" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2392" class="Bound">_</a> <a id="2394" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2396" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2381" class="Bound">B</a><a id="2397" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="2402" class="Comment">-- Sum types as inductive types</a>

## Equational Reasoning

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3541" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="EquationalReasoning"></a><a id="3548" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3548" class="Module">EquationalReasoning</a> <a id="3568" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3569" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3569" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="3571" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3573" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3574" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3574" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3576" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3578" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="3583" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3569" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="3585" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3587" class="Keyword">where</a>

## Actions on paths I

Properties and structure of the equality type.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="4137" class="Comment">-- Equality.</a>

<a id="4151" class="Comment">-- Types are higher groupoids.  If we see equalities as paths, this</a>
<a id="4219" class="Comment">-- is the inverse of a path. If we see equalities classically, this</a>
<a id="4287" class="Comment">-- is the symmetric property of equality.</a>
<a id="inv"></a><a id="4329" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4329" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="4333" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4335" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="4337" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4337" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="4338" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4340" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4341" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4341" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="4343" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4345" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="4350" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4337" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="4351" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="4354" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4355" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4355" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="4357" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4357" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="4359" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4361" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4341" class="Bound">A</a><a id="4362" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="4366" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4368" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4355" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="4370" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3301" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="4373" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4357" class="Bound">b</a>
  <a id="4377" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4379" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4357" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="4381" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3301" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="4384" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4355" class="Bound">a</a>
<a id="4386" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4329" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="4390" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4391" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3348" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="4396" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4396" class="Bound">a</a><a id="4397" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4399" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4401" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3348" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="4406" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4396" class="Bound">a</a>

<a id="4409" class="Comment">-- Functions are functors to equalities.  In other words, functions</a>
<a id="4477" class="Comment">-- preserve equalities.</a>

## Properties on the groupoid
Some properties on the groupoid structure of equalities

<a id="5630" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="5635" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4741" class="Module">·-Properties</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Transport

When we transport a proof of `(P a)` over an equality `(a == b)`, we
get a proof of `(P b)`.

    <a id="10671" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10672" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10672" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="10674" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10676" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10651" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="10678" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10680" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10653" class="Bound">D</a><a id="10681" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10683" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10685" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10686" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10686" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="10688" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10690" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10649" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="10692" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10694" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10651" class="Bound">C</a><a id="10695" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10697" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10699" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10700" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10700" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="10702" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10704" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10647" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="10706" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10708" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10649" class="Bound">B</a><a id="10709" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10711" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="10717" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="10719" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10672" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="10721" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3043" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="10723" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10686" class="Bound">g</a><a id="10724" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10726" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3043" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="10728" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10700" class="Bound">f</a><a id="10729" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10731" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3301" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="10734" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10735" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10672" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="10737" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3043" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="10739" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10740" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10686" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="10742" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3043" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="10744" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10700" class="Bound">f</a><a id="10745" class="Symbol">))</a>
  <a id="10750" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10630" class="Function">∘-rassoc</a> <a id="10759" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10759" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="10761" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10761" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="10763" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10763" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="10765" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10767" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4329" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="10771" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10772" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10465" class="Function">∘-lassoc</a> <a id="10781" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10759" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="10783" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10761" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="10785" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10763" class="Bound">f</a><a id="10786" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="10789" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="10794" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10425" class="Module">Composition</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Homotopy

In a type-theoretical sense, a homotopy between two
functions is a family of equalities between their applications.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10961" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Homotopy"></a><a id="10968" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10968" class="Module">Homotopy</a> <a id="10977" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10978" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10978" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="10981" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10981" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="10983" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10985" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10986" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10986" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="10988" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10990" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="10995" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10978" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="10997" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10999" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11000" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11000" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="11002" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11004" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10986" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="11006" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11008" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="11013" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10981" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="11015" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11017" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="11025" class="Comment">-- A homotopy is a natural isomorphism between two functions, we will write</a>
  <a id="11103" class="Comment">-- f ∼ g when (f x == g x) for all x.</a>
  <a id="Homotopy.homotopy"></a><a id="11143" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11143" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="11152" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11154" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11155" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11155" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11157" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11157" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="11159" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11161" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="11163" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11163" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="11165" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11167" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10986" class="Bound">A</a><a id="11168" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11170" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11172" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11000" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="11174" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11163" class="Bound">x</a><a id="11175" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="11178" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11180" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="11185" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11186" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10978" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="11189" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="11191" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10981" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="11193" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="11197" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11143" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="11206" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11206" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11208" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11208" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="11210" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11212" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11213" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11213" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="11215" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11217" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10986" class="Bound">A</a><a id="11218" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11220" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11222" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11206" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11224" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11213" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="11226" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3301" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="11229" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11208" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="11231" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11213" class="Bound">x</a>

  <a id="Homotopy._∼_"></a><a id="11236" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11236" class="Function Operator">_∼_</a> <a id="11240" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11242" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11243" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11243" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11245" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11245" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="11247" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11249" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="11251" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11251" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="11253" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11255" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10986" class="Bound">A</a><a id="11256" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11258" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11260" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11000" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="11262" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11251" class="Bound">x</a><a id="11263" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="11266" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11268" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="11273" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11274" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10978" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="11277" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="11279" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10981" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="11281" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="11285" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11285" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11287" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11236" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="11289" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11289" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="11291" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11293" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11143" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="11302" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11285" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11304" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11289" class="Bound">g</a>

  <a id="11309" class="Comment">-- Homotopy is an equivalence relation</a>
  <a id="Homotopy.h-refl"></a><a id="11350" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11350" class="Function">h-refl</a> <a id="11357" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11359" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11360" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11360" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11362" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11364" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11365" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11365" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="11367" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11369" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#10986" class="Bound">A</a><a id="11370" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11372" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11374" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11000" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="11376" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11365" class="Bound">x</a><a id="11377" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11379" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11381" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11360" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11383" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11236" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="11385" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11360" class="Bound">f</a>

<a id="12207" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="12212" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#11774" class="Module">HomotopyComposition</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Naturality

Homotopy is natural, meaning that it satisfies the following
square commutative diagram.

## Fibers

Contractible types with a center of contraction.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="13587" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Fibers"></a><a id="13594" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#13594" class="Module">Fibers</a> <a id="13601" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13602" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#13602" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="13605" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#13605" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="13607" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13609" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13610" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#13610" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="13612" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13614" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="13619" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#13602" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="13621" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13623" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13624" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#13624" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="13626" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13628" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="13633" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#13605" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="13635" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="13638" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="13647" class="Comment">-- The fiber of a map over a point is given by</a>

## Contractible types

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14116" class="Comment">-- Contractible.  Contractible types with a center of contraction.</a>

## Equivalence in HoTT

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14493" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Equivalence"></a><a id="14500" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14500" class="Module">Equivalence</a> <a id="14512" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="14521" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="DefinitionOfEquivalence"></a><a id="14528" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14528" class="Module">DefinitionOfEquivalence</a> <a id="14552" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14553" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14553" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="14556" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14556" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14558" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14560" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14561" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14561" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14563" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14565" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14570" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14553" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="14572" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14574" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14575" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14575" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14577" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14579" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14584" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14556" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14586" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14588" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="14598" class="Comment">-- Contractible maps. A map is contractible if the fiber in any</a>
    <a id="14666" class="Comment">-- point is contractible, that is, each element has a unique</a>
    <a id="14731" class="Comment">-- preimage.</a>
    <a id="Equivalence.DefinitionOfEquivalence.isContrMap"></a><a id="14748" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14748" class="Function">isContrMap</a> <a id="14759" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14761" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14762" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14762" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14764" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14766" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14561" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14768" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14770" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14575" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14771" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14773" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14775" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14780" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14781" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14553" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="14784" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="14786" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14556" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14788" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="14794" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14748" class="Function">isContrMap</a> <a id="14805" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14805" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14807" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14809" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14810" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14810" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="14812" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14814" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14575" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14815" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14817" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14819" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14333" class="Function">isContr</a> <a id="14827" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14828" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#13696" class="Function">fib</a> <a id="14832" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14805" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14834" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14810" class="Bound">b</a><a id="14835" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="14842" class="Comment">-- There exists an equivalence between two types if there exists a</a>
    <a id="14913" class="Comment">-- contractible function between them.</a>
    <a id="Equivalence.DefinitionOfEquivalence.isEquiv"></a><a id="14956" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14956" class="Function">isEquiv</a> <a id="14964" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14966" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14967" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14967" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14969" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14971" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14561" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14973" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14975" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14575" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14976" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14978" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14980" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14985" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14986" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14553" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="14989" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="14991" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14556" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14993" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="14999" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14956" class="Function">isEquiv</a> <a id="15007" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15009" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14748" class="Function">isContrMap</a>

## Cartesian Product

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="18265" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="CartesianProduct"></a><a id="18272" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18272" class="Module">CartesianProduct</a> <a id="18289" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18290" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18290" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="18293" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18293" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="18295" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18297" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18298" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18298" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18300" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18302" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="18307" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18290" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="18309" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18311" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18312" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18312" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="18314" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18316" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="18321" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18293" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="18323" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18325" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="18334" class="Comment">-- In a pair, the equality of the two components of the pairs is</a>
  <a id="18401" class="Comment">-- equivalent to equality of the two pairs.</a>
  <a id="CartesianProduct.prodComponentwise"></a><a id="18447" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18447" class="Function">prodComponentwise</a> <a id="18465" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18467" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18468" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18468" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18470" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18470" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="18472" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18474" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18298" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18476" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2315" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="18478" href="{% endraw %}{% link ## DecidableEquality

A type has decidable equality if any two of its
elements are equal or different. This would be a particular
instance of the Law of Excluded Middle that holds even if we do not
assume Excluded Middle.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="19450" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="DecidableEquality"></a><a id="19457" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19457" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a> <a id="19475" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19476" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19476" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="19477" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19479" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="19488" class="Comment">-- A type has decidable equality if we can prove that any two of its</a>
  <a id="19559" class="Comment">-- elements are equal or different.</a>
  <a id="DecidableEquality.decEq"></a><a id="19597" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19597" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="19603" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19605" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19606" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19606" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="19608" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19610" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="19615" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19476" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="19616" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19618" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19620" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="19625" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19476" class="Bound">ℓ</a>

<a id="20162" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20167" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19457" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Propositions

Propositions as described on the main text. A type
is a proposition if we can create a function making any two of its
elements equal. We create a type of propositions.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="20397" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Propositions"></a><a id="20404" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20404" class="Module">Propositions</a> <a id="20417" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="20426" class="Comment">-- A type is a mere proposition if any two inhabitants of the type</a>
  <a id="20495" class="Comment">-- are equal</a>
  <a id="Propositions.isProp"></a><a id="20510" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20510" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="20517" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20519" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="20521" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20521" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="20522" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="20525" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20526" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20526" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20528" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20530" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="20535" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20521" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="20536" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20538" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20540" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="20545" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20521" class="Bound">ℓ</a>
  <a id="20549" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20510" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="20556" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20556" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20558" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20560" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="20562" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20562" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="20564" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20564" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="20566" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20568" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20556" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20569" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20571" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20573" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20562" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="20575" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3301" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="20578" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20564" class="Bound">y</a><a id="20579" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="20584" class="Comment">-- The type of mere propositions</a>
  <a id="Propositions.hProp"></a><a id="20619" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20619" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="20625" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20627" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="20629" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20629" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="20630" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20632" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20634" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="20639" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20640" href="Agda.Primitive.html#627" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="20645" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20629" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="20646" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="20650" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20619" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="20656" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20657" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20657" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="20658" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20660" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20662" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2118" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="20664" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20665" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="20670" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20657" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="20671" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20673" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20510" class="Function">isProp</a>


  <a id="20684" class="Comment">-- The dependent function type to proposition types is itself a</a>
  <a id="20750" class="Comment">-- proposition.</a>
  <a id="Propositions.piProp"></a><a id="20768" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20768" class="Function">piProp</a> <a id="20775" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20777" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="20779" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20779" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="20782" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20782" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="20784" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20786" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20788" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20789" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20789" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20791" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20793" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="20798" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20779" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="20800" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20802" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20804" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20805" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20805" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="20807" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20809" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20789" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20811" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20813" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="20818" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20782" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="20820" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="20831" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20833" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="20835" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20835" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="20837" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20839" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20789" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20840" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20842" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20844" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20510" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="20851" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20852" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20805" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="20854" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20835" class="Bound">a</a><a id="20855" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="20858" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20860" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20510" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="20867" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="20869" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20869" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="20871" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20873" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20789" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20874" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20876" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20878" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20805" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="20880" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20869" class="Bound">a</a><a id="20881" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="20885" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20768" class="Function">piProp</a> <a id="20892" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20892" class="Bound">props</a> <a id="20898" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20898" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="20900" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20900" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="20902" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20904" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#16595" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="20911" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="20913" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20913" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="20915" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20917" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20892" class="Bound">props</a> <a id="20923" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20913" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="20925" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20926" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20898" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="20928" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20913" class="Bound">a</a><a id="20929" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20931" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20932" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20900" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="20934" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20913" class="Bound">a</a><a id="20935" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="Propositions.isProp-prod"></a><a id="20998" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20998" class="Function">isProp-prod</a> <a id="21010" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21012" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="21014" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21014" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="21017" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21017" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="21019" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21021" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21023" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21024" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21024" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="21026" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21028" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="21033" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21014" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="21035" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21037" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21039" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21040" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21040" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="21042" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21044" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="21049" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21017" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="21051" class="Symbol">}</a>

## Sets

Sets are types without any higher dimensional structure, all
parallel paths are homotopic and the homotopy is given by a
continuous function on the two paths.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="21381" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Sets"></a><a id="21388" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21388" class="Module">Sets</a> <a id="21393" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="21402" class="Comment">-- A type is a &quot;set&quot; by definition if any two equalities on the type</a>
  <a id="21473" class="Comment">-- are equal.</a>

<a id="22110" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="22115" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21388" class="Module">Sets</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## HLevels

Higher levels of the homotopical structure, where the
first levels are:

- Contractible types (0)
- Propositions (1)
- Sets (2)

They would correspond to homotopy levels. We only work with
these first levels.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="22368" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="HLevels"></a><a id="22375" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22375" class="Module">HLevels</a> <a id="22383" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="22392" class="Comment">-- Propositions are Sets.</a>

## EquivalenceProp

Equivalence of two types is a proposition
Moreover, equivalences preserve propositions.

<a id="24378" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="24383" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23596" class="Module">EquivalenceProp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Half-Adjoints

Half-adjoints are an auxiliary notion that helps us
to define a suitable notion of equivalence, meaning that it is a
proposition and that it captures the usual notion of equivalence.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="24627" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Halfadjoints"></a><a id="24634" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24634" class="Module">Halfadjoints</a> <a id="24647" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24648" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24648" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="24651" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24651" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24653" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24655" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24656" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24656" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24658" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24660" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24665" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24648" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="24667" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24669" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24670" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24670" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24672" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24674" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24679" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24651" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24681" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24683" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="24692" class="Comment">-- Half adjoint equivalence.</a>

            <a id="27170" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3907" class="Function Operator">∎</a>

<a id="27305" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="27310" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24634" class="Module">Halfadjoints</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Quasiinverses

Two functions are quasiinverses if we can construct
a function providing gfx = x and fgy = y for any given x and y.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="27484" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Quasiinverses"></a><a id="27491" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#27491" class="Module">Quasiinverses</a> <a id="27505" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27506" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#27506" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="27509" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#27509" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="27511" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="27513" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27514" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#27514" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="27516" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27518" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="27523" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#27506" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="27525" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="27527" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27528" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#27528" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="27530" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27532" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#802" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="27537" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#27509" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="27539" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="27541" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="30237" class="Comment">-- Half-adjoint equivalences are quasiinverses.</a>

   <a id="31645" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3962" class="Function Operator">begin</a>
     <a id="31656" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2218" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="31660" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31661" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31102" class="Function">compEqv</a> <a id="31669" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31628" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="31671" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31672" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31314" class="Function">invEqv</a> <a id="31679" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31628" class="Bound">α</a><a id="31680" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="31683" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3808" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="31687" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3348" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="31692" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="31694" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3808" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
     <a id="31701" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2218" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="31705" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31706" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31314" class="Function">invEqv</a> <a id="31713" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31628" class="Bound">α</a><a id="31714" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31716" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3043" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="31718" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2218" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="31722" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31628" class="Bound">α</a>     <a id="31728" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3808" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="31732" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#16595" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="31739" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31740" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15864" class="Function">rlmap-inverse-h</a> <a id="31756" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31628" class="Bound">α</a><a id="31757" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31759" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3808" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
     <a id="31766" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2987" class="Function">id</a>
   <a id="31772" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3907" class="Function Operator">∎</a><a id="31773" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="31776" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="31781" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#30522" class="Module">EquivalenceComposition</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Univalence

Voevodsky's univalence axiom is postulated. It induces
an equality between any two equivalent types. Some β and η rules
are provided.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="31980" class="Comment">-- module Univalence where</a>
<a id="32007" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="32010" class="Comment">--   -- Voevodsky&#39;s Univalence Axiom.</a>
<a id="32048" class="Comment">--   module UnivalenceAxiom {ℓ} {A B : Type ℓ} where</a>
<a id="32101" class="Comment">--     idtoeqv : A == B → A ≃ B</a>
<a id="32133" class="Comment">--     idtoeqv p = qinv-≃</a>
<a id="32159" class="Comment">--       (transport (λ x → x) p)</a>
<a id="32192" class="Comment">--       (transport (λ x → x) (inv p) , (transport-inv-l p , transport-inv-r p))</a>
<a id="32273" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="32276" class="Comment">--     -- The Univalence axiom induces an equivalence between equalities</a>
<a id="32349" class="Comment">--     -- and equivalences.</a>
<a id="32377" class="Comment">--     postulate axiomUnivalence : isEquiv idtoeqv</a>
<a id="32428" class="Comment">--     eqvUnivalence : (A == B) ≃ (A ≃ B)</a>
<a id="32470" class="Comment">--     eqvUnivalence = idtoeqv , axiomUnivalence</a>
<a id="32519" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="32522" class="Comment">--     -- Introduction rule for equalities.</a>
<a id="32566" class="Comment">--     ua : A ≃ B → A == B</a>
<a id="32593" class="Comment">--     ua = remap eqvUnivalence</a>
<a id="32625" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="32628" class="Comment">--     -- Computation rules</a>
<a id="32656" class="Comment">--     ua-β : (eqv : A ≃ B) → idtoeqv (ua eqv) == eqv</a>
<a id="32710" class="Comment">--     ua-β eqv = lrmap-inverse eqvUnivalence</a>
<a id="32756" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="32759" class="Comment">--     ua-η : (p : A == B) → ua (idtoeqv p) == p</a>
<a id="32808" class="Comment">--     ua-η p = rlmap-inverse eqvUnivalence</a>
<a id="32852" class="Comment">--   open UnivalenceAxiom public</a>
<a id="32885" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="32888" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="32891" class="Comment">--   module UnivalenceLemmas {ℓ} where</a>
<a id="32930" class="Comment">--     -- The identity equivalence creates the trivial path.</a>
<a id="32991" class="Comment">--     ua-id : {A : Type ℓ} → ua idEqv == refl A</a>
<a id="33040" class="Comment">--     ua-id {A} =</a>
<a id="33059" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="33074" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv              ==⟨ ap ua (sameEqv (refl id)) ⟩</a>
<a id="33139" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (refl A)) ==⟨ ua-η (refl A) ⟩</a>
<a id="33192" class="Comment">--         refl A</a>
<a id="33210" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="33221" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="33224" class="Comment">--     -- The composition of equivalences is preserved into composition</a>
<a id="33296" class="Comment">--     -- of equalities.</a>
<a id="33321" class="Comment">--     ua-comp : {A B C : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → (β : B ≃ C) → ua (compEqv α β) == ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="33417" class="Comment">--     ua-comp α β =</a>
<a id="33438" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="33453" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α β)                               ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv x β)) (inv (ua-β α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="33560" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) β)                ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) x))</a>
<a id="33665" class="Comment">--                                                            (inv (ua-β β)) ⟩</a>
<a id="33744" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β))) ==⟨ ap ua lemma ⟩</a>
<a id="33820" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))                     ==⟨ ua-η (ua α · ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="33903" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="33926" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="33937" class="Comment">--       where</a>
<a id="33952" class="Comment">--         lemma : compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β)) == idtoeqv (ua α · ua β)</a>
<a id="34038" class="Comment">--         lemma = sameEqv (</a>
<a id="34067" class="Comment">--           begin</a>
<a id="34086" class="Comment">--             fst (idtoeqv (ua β)) ∘ fst (idtoeqv (ua α))                 ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="34174" class="Comment">--             (transport (λ x → x) (ua β)) ∘ (transport (λ x → x) (ua α)) ==⟨ transport-comp (ua α) (ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="34284" class="Comment">--             transport (λ x → x) (ua α · ua β)                           ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="34372" class="Comment">--             fst (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))</a>
<a id="34415" class="Comment">--           ∎)</a>
<a id="34431" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="34434" class="Comment">--     -- Inverses are preserved.</a>
<a id="34468" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua α · ua (invEqv α) == refl A</a>
<a id="34548" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r α =</a>
<a id="34568" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="34583" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua (invEqv α)      ==⟨ inv (ua-comp α (invEqv α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="34653" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α (invEqv α)) ==⟨ ap ua (compEqv-inv α) ⟩</a>
<a id="34718" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv                  ==⟨ ua-id ⟩</a>
<a id="34767" class="Comment">--         refl _</a>
<a id="34785" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="34796" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="34799" class="Comment">--     ua-inv : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua (invEqv α) == inv (ua α)</a>
<a id="34874" class="Comment">--     ua-inv α =</a>
<a id="34892" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="34907" class="Comment">--         ua (invEqv α)                       ==⟨ ap (_· ua (invEqv α)) (inv (·-linv (ua α))) ⟩</a>
<a id="35004" class="Comment">--         inv (ua α) · ua α · ua (invEqv α)   ==⟨ ·-assoc (inv (ua α)) _ _ ⟩</a>
<a id="35082" class="Comment">--         inv (ua α) · (ua α · ua (invEqv α)) ==⟨ ap (inv (ua α) ·_) (ua-inv-r α) ⟩</a>
<a id="35167" class="Comment">--         inv (ua α) · refl _                 ==⟨ inv (·-runit (inv ((ua α)))) ⟩</a>
<a id="35249" class="Comment">--         inv (ua α)</a>
<a id="35271" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="35282" class="Comment">--   open UnivalenceLemmas public</a>
<a id="35316" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="35319" class="Comment">-- open Univalence</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
